<span data-ttu-id="8024c-627">A saída do console do aplicativo, mostrando todos os erros, é canalizada para o console do Kudu.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-627">The console output from the app, showing any errors, is piped to the Kudu console.</span></span>

### <a name="aspnet-core-module-stdout-log-azure-app-service"></a><span data-ttu-id="8024c-628">Log de stdout do módulo ASP.NET Core (serviço Azure App)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-628">ASP.NET Core Module stdout log (Azure App Service)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8024c-629">O log de stdout do Módulo do ASP.NET Core geralmente registra mensagens de erro úteis não encontradas no Log de Eventos do Aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-629">The ASP.NET Core Module stdout log often records useful error messages not found in the Application Event Log.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8024c-630">Para habilitar e exibir logs de stdout:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-630">To enable and view stdout logs:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="8024c-631">Navegue até a folha **Diagnosticar e resolver problemas** no portal do Azure.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-631">Navigate to the **Diagnose and solve problems** blade in the Azure portal.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="8024c-632">Em **SELECIONAR CATEGORIA DE PROBLEMA** , selecione o botão **Aplicativo Web Inoperante** .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-632">Under **SELECT PROBLEM CATEGORY** , select the **Web App Down** button.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="8024c-633">Em **Soluções Sugeridas** > **Habilitar o Redirecionamento de Log de Stdout** , selecione o botão para **Abrir o Console do Kudu para editar o Web.Config** .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-633">Under **Suggested Solutions** > **Enable Stdout Log Redirection** , select the button to **Open Kudu Console to edit Web.Config** .</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="8024c-634">No **Console de Diagnóstico** do Kudu, abra as pastas no caminho **site** > **wwwroot** .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-634">In the Kudu **Diagnostic Console** , open the folders to the path **site** > **wwwroot** .</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8024c-635">Role para baixo para revelar o arquivo *web.config* na parte inferior da lista.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-635">Scroll down to reveal the *web.config* file at the bottom of the list.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="8024c-636">Clique no ícone de lápis ao lado do arquivo *web.config* .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-636">Click the pencil icon next to the *web.config* file.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="8024c-637">Defina **stdoutLogEnabled** para `true` e altere o caminho **stdoutLogFile** para `\\?\%home%\LogFiles\stdout`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-637">Set **stdoutLogEnabled** to `true` and change the **stdoutLogFile** path to: `\\?\%home%\LogFiles\stdout`.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="8024c-638">Selecione **Salvar** para salvar o arquivo *web.config* atualizado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-638">Select **Save** to save the updated *web.config* file.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="8024c-639">Faça uma solicitação ao aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-639">Make a request to the app.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="8024c-640">Retorne ao portal do Azure.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-640">Return to the Azure portal.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8024c-641">Selecione a folha **Ferramentas Avançadas** na área **FERRAMENTAS DE DESENVOLVIMENTO** .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-641">Select the **Advanced Tools** blade in the **DEVELOPMENT TOOLS** area.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8024c-642">Selecione o **botão &rarr; ir** .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-642">Select the **Go&rarr;** button.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8024c-643">O console do Kudu é aberto em uma nova janela ou guia do navegador.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-643">The Kudu console opens in a new browser tab or window.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="8024c-644">Usando a barra de navegação na parte superior da página, abra **Console de depuração** e selecione **CMD** .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-644">Using the navigation bar at the top of the page, open **Debug console** and select **CMD** .</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="8024c-645">Abra a pasta **LogFiles** .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-645">Select the **LogFiles** folder.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="8024c-646">Inspecione a coluna **Modificado em** e selecione o ícone de lápis para editar o log de stdout com a data da última modificação.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-646">Inspect the **Modified** column and select the pencil icon to edit the stdout log with the latest modification date.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="8024c-647">Quando o arquivo de log é aberto, o erro é exibido.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-647">When the log file opens, the error is displayed.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8024c-648">Desabilite o registro em log de stdout quando a solução de problemas for concluída:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-648">Disable stdout logging when troubleshooting is complete:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="8024c-649">No **Console de Diagnóstico** do Kudu, retorne para o caminho **site** > **wwwroot** para revelar o arquivo *web.config* .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-649">In the Kudu **Diagnostic Console** , return to the path **site** > **wwwroot** to reveal the *web.config* file.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8024c-650">Abra o arquivo **web.config** novamente, selecionando o ícone de lápis.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-650">Open the **web.config** file again by selecting the pencil icon.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="8024c-651">Defina **stdoutLogEnabled** para `false`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-651">Set **stdoutLogEnabled** to `false`.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="8024c-652">Selecione **Salvar** para salvar o arquivo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-652">Select **Save** to save the file.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8024c-653">Para obter mais informações, consulte <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#log-creation-and-redirection>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-653">For more information, see <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#log-creation-and-redirection>.</span></span>

> [!WARNING]
> <span data-ttu-id="8024c-654">Falha ao desabilitar o log de stdout pode levar a falhas de aplicativo ou de servidor.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-654">Failure to disable the stdout log can lead to app or server failure.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8024c-655">Não há limites para o tamanho do arquivo de log ou para o número de arquivos de log criados.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-655">There's no limit on log file size or the number of log files created.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8024c-656">Somente use o log de stdout para solucionar problemas de inicialização de aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-656">Only use stdout logging to troubleshoot app startup problems.</span></span>
>
> <span data-ttu-id="8024c-657">Para registro em log geral em um aplicativo ASP.NET Core após a inicialização, use uma biblioteca de registro em log que limita o tamanho do arquivo de log e realiza a rotação de logs.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-657">For general logging in an ASP.NET Core app after startup, use a logging library that limits log file size and rotates logs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8024c-658">Para obter mais informações, veja [provedores de log de terceiros](xref:fundamentals/logging/index#third-party-logging-providers).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-658">For more information, see [third-party logging providers](xref:fundamentals/logging/index#third-party-logging-providers).</span></span>

### <a name="aspnet-core-module-debug-log-azure-app-service"></a><span data-ttu-id="8024c-659">Log de depuração do módulo ASP.NET Core (serviço Azure App)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-659">ASP.NET Core Module debug log (Azure App Service)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8024c-660">O log de depuração do Módulo do ASP.NET Core fornece registro em log adicional e mais profundo do Módulo do ASP.NET Core.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-660">The ASP.NET Core Module debug log provides additional, deeper logging from the ASP.NET Core Module.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8024c-661">Para habilitar e exibir logs de stdout:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-661">To enable and view stdout logs:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="8024c-662">Para habilitar o log de diagnóstico avançado, execute um destes procedimentos:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-662">To enable the enhanced diagnostic log, perform either of the following:</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="8024c-663">Siga as instruções em [Logs de diagnóstico avançados](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#enhanced-diagnostic-logs) para configurar o aplicativo para um log de diagnósticos avançado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-663">Follow the instructions in [Enhanced diagnostic logs](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#enhanced-diagnostic-logs) to configure the app for an enhanced diagnostic logging.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8024c-664">Reimplante o aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-664">Redeploy the app.</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="8024c-665">Adicione a `<handlerSettings>` mostrada em [Logs de diagnóstico avançados](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#enhanced-diagnostic-logs) para o arquivo *web.config* do aplicativo ao vivo usando o console do Kudu:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-665">Add the `<handlerSettings>` shown in [Enhanced diagnostic logs](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#enhanced-diagnostic-logs) to the live app's *web.config* file using the Kudu console:</span></span>
     1. <span data-ttu-id="8024c-666">Abra **Ferramentas Avançadas** na área **Ferramentas de Desenvolvimento** .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-666">Open **Advanced Tools** in the **Development Tools** area.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8024c-667">Selecione o **botão &rarr; ir** .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-667">Select the **Go&rarr;** button.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8024c-668">O console do Kudu é aberto em uma nova janela ou guia do navegador.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-668">The Kudu console opens in a new browser tab or window.</span></span>
     1. <span data-ttu-id="8024c-669">Usando a barra de navegação na parte superior da página, abra **Console de depuração** e selecione **CMD** .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-669">Using the navigation bar at the top of the page, open **Debug console** and select **CMD** .</span></span>
     1. <span data-ttu-id="8024c-670">Abra as pastas no caminho **site**  >  **wwwroot** .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-670">Open the folders to the path **site** > **wwwroot** .</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8024c-671">Edite o arquivo *web.config* selecionando o botão de lápis.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-671">Edit the *web.config* file by selecting the pencil button.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8024c-672">Adicione a seção `<handlerSettings>` conforme mostrado em [Logs de diagnóstico avançados](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#enhanced-diagnostic-logs).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-672">Add the `<handlerSettings>` section as shown in [Enhanced diagnostic logs](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#enhanced-diagnostic-logs).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8024c-673">Selecione o botão **Salvar** .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-673">Select the **Save** button.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="8024c-674">Abra **Ferramentas Avançadas** na área **Ferramentas de Desenvolvimento** .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-674">Open **Advanced Tools** in the **Development Tools** area.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8024c-675">Selecione o **botão &rarr; ir** .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-675">Select the **Go&rarr;** button.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8024c-676">O console do Kudu é aberto em uma nova janela ou guia do navegador.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-676">The Kudu console opens in a new browser tab or window.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="8024c-677">Usando a barra de navegação na parte superior da página, abra **Console de depuração** e selecione **CMD** .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-677">Using the navigation bar at the top of the page, open **Debug console** and select **CMD** .</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="8024c-678">Abra as pastas no caminho **site**  >  **wwwroot** .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-678">Open the folders to the path **site** > **wwwroot** .</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8024c-679">Se você não fornecer um caminho para o arquivo *aspnetcore-debug.log* , o arquivo aparecerá na lista.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-679">If you didn't supply a path for the *aspnetcore-debug.log* file, the file appears in the list.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8024c-680">Se você tiver fornecido um caminho, navegue até o local do arquivo de log.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-680">If you supplied a path, navigate to the location of the log file.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8024c-682">Desabilite o registro em log de depuração quando a solução de problemas for concluída:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-682">Disable debug logging when troubleshooting is complete:</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8024c-687">Para obter mais informações, consulte <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#enhanced-diagnostic-logs>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-687">For more information, see <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#enhanced-diagnostic-logs>.</span></span>

> <span data-ttu-id="8024c-691">Para registro em log geral em um aplicativo ASP.NET Core após a inicialização, use uma biblioteca de registro em log que limita o tamanho do arquivo de log e realiza a rotação de logs.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-691">For general logging in an ASP.NET Core app after startup, use a logging library that limits log file size and rotates logs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8024c-692">Para obter mais informações, veja [provedores de log de terceiros](xref:fundamentals/logging/index#third-party-logging-providers).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-692">For more information, see [third-party logging providers](xref:fundamentals/logging/index#third-party-logging-providers).</span></span>

### <a name="monitoring-blades"></a><span data-ttu-id="8024c-697">Folhas de monitoramento</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-697">Monitoring blades</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8024c-726">Sempre desabilite o registro em log de stdout após concluir a solução de problemas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-726">Be sure to disable stdout logging when troubleshooting is complete.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8024c-727">Para exibir os logs de rastreamento de solicitação com falha (logs FREB):</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-727">To view the failed request tracing logs (FREB logs):</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8024c-730">Confira a [seção de Rastreamentos de solicitação com falha no tópico Habilitar o log de diagnósticos para aplicativos Web no Serviço de Aplicativo do Azure](/azure/app-service/web-sites-enable-diagnostic-log#failed-request-traces) e as [Perguntas frequentes do desempenho do aplicativo para Aplicativos Web no Azure: como ativar o rastreamento de solicitação com falha?](/azure/app-service/app-service-web-availability-performance-application-issues-faq#how-do-i-turn-on-failed-request-tracing) para obter mais informações.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-730">See [Failed request traces section of the Enable diagnostics logging for web apps in Azure App Service topic](/azure/app-service/web-sites-enable-diagnostic-log#failed-request-traces) and the [Application performance FAQs for Web Apps in Azure: How do I turn on failed request tracing?](/azure/app-service/app-service-web-availability-performance-application-issues-faq#how-do-i-turn-on-failed-request-tracing) for more information.</span></span>

>
> <span data-ttu-id="8024c-734">Para registro em log de rotina em um aplicativo ASP.NET Core, use uma biblioteca de registro em log que limita o tamanho do arquivo de log e realiza a rotação de logs.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-734">For routine logging in an ASP.NET Core app, use a logging library that limits log file size and rotates logs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8024c-735">Para obter mais informações, veja [provedores de log de terceiros](xref:fundamentals/logging/index#third-party-logging-providers).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-735">For more information, see [third-party logging providers](xref:fundamentals/logging/index#third-party-logging-providers).</span></span>

## <a name="troubleshoot-on-iis"></a><span data-ttu-id="8024c-736">Solução de problemas no IIS</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-736">Troubleshoot on IIS</span></span>

### <a name="application-event-log-iis"></a><span data-ttu-id="8024c-737">Log de eventos do aplicativo (IIS)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-737">Application Event Log (IIS)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8024c-738">Acesse o Log de Eventos do Aplicativo:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-738">Access the Application Event Log:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="8024c-739">Abra o menu Iniciar, procure *Visualizador de eventos* e selecione o aplicativo **Visualizador de eventos** .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-739">Open the Start menu, search for *Event Viewer* , and select the **Event Viewer** app.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="8024c-740">No **Visualizador de Eventos** , abra o nó **Logs do Windows** .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-740">In **Event Viewer** , open the **Windows Logs** node.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="8024c-741">Selecione **Aplicativo** para abrir o Log de Eventos do Aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-741">Select **Application** to open the Application Event Log.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="8024c-742">Procure erros associados ao aplicativo com falha.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-742">Search for errors associated with the failing app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8024c-743">Os erros têm um valor *Módulo AspNetCore do IIS* ou *Módulo AspNetCore do IIS Express* na coluna *Origem* .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-743">Errors have a value of *IIS AspNetCore Module* or *IIS Express AspNetCore Module* in the *Source* column.</span></span>

### <a name="run-the-app-at-a-command-prompt"></a><span data-ttu-id="8024c-744">Execute o aplicativo em um prompt de comando</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-744">Run the app at a command prompt</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8024c-745">Muitos erros de inicialização não produzem informações úteis no Log de Eventos do Aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-745">Many startup errors don't produce useful information in the Application Event Log.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8024c-746">Você pode encontrar a causa de alguns erros ao executar o aplicativo em um prompt de comando no sistema de hospedagem.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-746">You can find the cause of some errors by running the app at a command prompt on the hosting system.</span></span>

#### <a name="framework-dependent-deployment"></a><span data-ttu-id="8024c-747">Implantação dependente de estrutura</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-747">Framework-dependent deployment</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8024c-748">Se o aplicativo é uma [implantação dependente de estrutura](/dotnet/core/deploying/#framework-dependent-deployments-fdd):</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-748">If the app is a [framework-dependent deployment](/dotnet/core/deploying/#framework-dependent-deployments-fdd):</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="8024c-749">Em um prompt de comando, navegue até a pasta de implantação e execute o aplicativo, executando o assembly do aplicativo com *dotnet.exe* .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-749">At a command prompt, navigate to the deployment folder and run the app by executing the app's assembly with *dotnet.exe* .</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8024c-750">No comando a seguir, substitua o nome do assembly do aplicativo por \<assembly_name> : `dotnet .\<assembly_name>.dll` .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-750">In the following command, substitute the name of the app's assembly for \<assembly_name>: `dotnet .\<assembly_name>.dll`.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="8024c-751">A saída do console do aplicativo, mostrando eventuais erros, é gravada na janela do console.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-751">The console output from the app, showing any errors, is written to the console window.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="8024c-752">Se os erros ocorrerem ao fazer uma solicitação para o aplicativo, faça uma solicitação para o host e a porta em que o Kestrel escuta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-752">If the errors occur when making a request to the app, make a request to the host and port where Kestrel listens.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8024c-753">Usando o host e a porta padrão, faça uma solicitação para `http://localhost:5000/`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-753">Using the default host and post, make a request to `http://localhost:5000/`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8024c-754">Se o aplicativo responde normalmente no endereço do ponto de extremidade do Kestrel, a probabilidade de o problema estar relacionado à configuração de hospedagem é maior e, de estar relacionado ao aplicativo, menor.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-754">If the app responds normally at the Kestrel endpoint address, the problem is more likely related to the hosting configuration and less likely within the app.</span></span>

#### <a name="self-contained-deployment"></a><span data-ttu-id="8024c-755">Implantação autocontida</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-755">Self-contained deployment</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8024c-756">Se o aplicativo é uma [implantação autossuficiente](/dotnet/core/deploying/#self-contained-deployments-scd):</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-756">If the app is a [self-contained deployment](/dotnet/core/deploying/#self-contained-deployments-scd):</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="8024c-757">Em um prompt de comando, navegue até a pasta de implantação e execute o arquivo executável do aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-757">At a command prompt, navigate to the deployment folder and run the app's executable.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8024c-758">No comando a seguir, substitua o nome do assembly do aplicativo por \<assembly_name> : `<assembly_name>.exe` .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-758">In the following command, substitute the name of the app's assembly for \<assembly_name>: `<assembly_name>.exe`.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="8024c-759">A saída do console do aplicativo, mostrando eventuais erros, é gravada na janela do console.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-759">The console output from the app, showing any errors, is written to the console window.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="8024c-760">Se os erros ocorrerem ao fazer uma solicitação para o aplicativo, faça uma solicitação para o host e a porta em que o Kestrel escuta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-760">If the errors occur when making a request to the app, make a request to the host and port where Kestrel listens.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8024c-761">Usando o host e a porta padrão, faça uma solicitação para `http://localhost:5000/`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-761">Using the default host and post, make a request to `http://localhost:5000/`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8024c-762">Se o aplicativo responde normalmente no endereço do ponto de extremidade do Kestrel, a probabilidade de o problema estar relacionado à configuração de hospedagem é maior e, de estar relacionado ao aplicativo, menor.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-762">If the app responds normally at the Kestrel endpoint address, the problem is more likely related to the hosting configuration and less likely within the app.</span></span>

### <a name="aspnet-core-module-stdout-log-iis"></a><span data-ttu-id="8024c-763">Log de stdout do módulo ASP.NET Core (IIS)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-763">ASP.NET Core Module stdout log (IIS)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8024c-764">Para habilitar e exibir logs de stdout:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-764">To enable and view stdout logs:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="8024c-765">Navegue até a pasta de implantação do site no sistema de hospedagem.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-765">Navigate to the site's deployment folder on the hosting system.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="8024c-766">Se a pasta *logs* não estiver presente, crie-a.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-766">If the *logs* folder isn't present, create the folder.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8024c-767">Para obter instruções sobre como habilitar o MSBuild para criar a pasta *logs* na implantação automaticamente, veja o tópico [Estrutura de diretórios](xref:host-and-deploy/directory-structure).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-767">For instructions on how to enable MSBuild to create the *logs* folder in the deployment automatically, see the [Directory structure](xref:host-and-deploy/directory-structure) topic.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="8024c-768">Edite o arquivo *web.config* .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-768">Edit the *web.config* file.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8024c-769">Defina **stdoutLogEnabled** para `true` e altere o caminho **stdoutLogFile** para apontar para a pasta *logs* (por exemplo, `.\logs\stdout`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-769">Set **stdoutLogEnabled** to `true` and change the **stdoutLogFile** path to point to the *logs* folder (for example, `.\logs\stdout`).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8024c-770">`stdout` no caminho é o prefixo do nome do arquivo de log.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-770">`stdout` in the path is the log file name prefix.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8024c-771">Uma extensão de arquivo, uma ID do processo e um carimbo de data/hora são adicionados automaticamente quando o log é criado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-771">A timestamp, process id, and file extension are added automatically when the log is created.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8024c-772">Usando `stdout` como o prefixo do nome do arquivo, um arquivo de log típico é nomeado *stdout_20180205184032_5412.log* .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-772">Using `stdout` as the file name prefix, a typical log file is named *stdout_20180205184032_5412.log* .</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="8024c-773">Verifique se a identidade do pool de aplicativos tem permissões de gravação para a pasta *logs* .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-773">Ensure your application pool's identity has write permissions to the *logs* folder.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="8024c-774">Salve o arquivo *web.config* atualizado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-774">Save the updated *web.config* file.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="8024c-775">Faça uma solicitação ao aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-775">Make a request to the app.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="8024c-776">Navegue até a pasta *logs* .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-776">Navigate to the *logs* folder.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8024c-777">Localize e abra o log de stdout mais recente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-777">Find and open the most recent stdout log.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="8024c-778">Estude o log em busca de erros.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-778">Study the log for errors.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8024c-779">Desabilite o registro em log de stdout quando a solução de problemas for concluída:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-779">Disable stdout logging when troubleshooting is complete:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="8024c-780">Edite o arquivo *web.config* .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-780">Edit the *web.config* file.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="8024c-781">Defina **stdoutLogEnabled** para `false`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-781">Set **stdoutLogEnabled** to `false`.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="8024c-782">Salve o arquivo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-782">Save the file.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8024c-783">Para obter mais informações, consulte <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#log-creation-and-redirection>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-783">For more information, see <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#log-creation-and-redirection>.</span></span>

> [!WARNING]
> <span data-ttu-id="8024c-784">Falha ao desabilitar o log de stdout pode levar a falhas de aplicativo ou de servidor.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-784">Failure to disable the stdout log can lead to app or server failure.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8024c-785">Não há limites para o tamanho do arquivo de log ou para o número de arquivos de log criados.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-785">There's no limit on log file size or the number of log files created.</span></span>
>
> <span data-ttu-id="8024c-786">Para registro em log de rotina em um aplicativo ASP.NET Core, use uma biblioteca de registro em log que limita o tamanho do arquivo de log e realiza a rotação de logs.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-786">For routine logging in an ASP.NET Core app, use a logging library that limits log file size and rotates logs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8024c-787">Para obter mais informações, veja [provedores de log de terceiros](xref:fundamentals/logging/index#third-party-logging-providers).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-787">For more information, see [third-party logging providers](xref:fundamentals/logging/index#third-party-logging-providers).</span></span>

### <a name="aspnet-core-module-debug-log-iis"></a><span data-ttu-id="8024c-788">Log de depuração do módulo ASP.NET Core (IIS)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-788">ASP.NET Core Module debug log (IIS)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8024c-789">Adicione as seguintes configurações de manipulador ao arquivo de *web.config* do aplicativo para habilitar ASP.NET Core log de depuração do módulo:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-789">Add the following handler settings to the app's *web.config* file to enable ASP.NET Core Module debug log:</span></span>

```xml
<aspNetCore ...>
  <handlerSettings>
    <handlerSetting name="debugLevel" value="file" />
    <handlerSetting name="debugFile" value="c:\temp\ancm.log" />
  </handlerSettings>
</aspNetCore>
```

<span data-ttu-id="8024c-790">Confirme se o caminho especificado para o log existe e se a identidade do pool de aplicativos tem permissões de gravação no local.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-790">Confirm that the path specified for the log exists and that the app pool's identity has write permissions to the location.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8024c-791">Para obter mais informações, consulte <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#enhanced-diagnostic-logs>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-791">For more information, see <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#enhanced-diagnostic-logs>.</span></span>

### <a name="enable-the-developer-exception-page"></a><span data-ttu-id="8024c-792">Habilitar a página de exceção do desenvolvedor</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-792">Enable the Developer Exception Page</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8024c-793">A  [variável de ambiente `ASPNETCORE_ENVIRONMENT` pode ser adicionada ao web.config](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#setting-environment-variables) para executar o aplicativo no ambiente de desenvolvimento.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-793">The `ASPNETCORE_ENVIRONMENT` [environment variable can be added to web.config](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#setting-environment-variables) to run the app in the Development environment.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8024c-794">Desde que o ambiente não seja substituído na inicialização do aplicativo por `UseEnvironment` no compilador do host, definir a variável de ambiente permite que a [Página de Exceções do Desenvolvedor](xref:fundamentals/error-handling) apareça quando o aplicativo é executado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-794">As long as the environment isn't overridden in app startup by `UseEnvironment` on the host builder, setting the environment variable allows the [Developer Exception Page](xref:fundamentals/error-handling) to appear when the app is run.</span></span>

```xml
<aspNetCore processPath="dotnet"
      arguments=".\MyApp.dll"
      stdoutLogEnabled="false"
      stdoutLogFile=".\logs\stdout"
      hostingModel="InProcess">
  <environmentVariables>
    <environmentVariable name="ASPNETCORE_ENVIRONMENT" value="Development" />
  </environmentVariables>
</aspNetCore>
```

<span data-ttu-id="8024c-795">Configurar a variável de ambiente para `ASPNETCORE_ENVIRONMENT` só é recomendado para servidores de preparo e de teste que não estejam expostos à Internet.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-795">Setting the environment variable for `ASPNETCORE_ENVIRONMENT` is only recommended for use on staging and testing servers that aren't exposed to the Internet.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8024c-796">Remova a variável de ambiente do arquivo *web.config* após a solução de problemas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-796">Remove the environment variable from the *web.config* file after troubleshooting.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8024c-797">Para obter informações sobre como definir variáveis de ambiente no *web.config* , confira [Elemento filho environmentVariables de aspNetCore](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#setting-environment-variables).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-797">For information on setting environment variables in *web.config* , see [environmentVariables child element of aspNetCore](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#setting-environment-variables).</span></span>

### <a name="obtain-data-from-an-app"></a><span data-ttu-id="8024c-798">Obter dados de um aplicativo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-798">Obtain data from an app</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8024c-799">Se um aplicativo for capaz de responder às solicitações, obtenha as solicitações, conexão e dados adicionais do aplicativo que usar o middleware embutido de terminal.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-799">If an app is capable of responding to requests, obtain request, connection, and additional data from the app using terminal inline middleware.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8024c-800">Para saber mais e obter um código de exemplo, consulte <xref:test/troubleshoot#obtain-data-from-an-app>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-800">For more information and sample code, see <xref:test/troubleshoot#obtain-data-from-an-app>.</span></span>

### <a name="slow-or-hanging-app-iis"></a><span data-ttu-id="8024c-801">Aplicativo lento ou suspenso (IIS)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-801">Slow or hanging app (IIS)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8024c-802">Um *despejo* é um instantâneo da memória do sistema e pode ajudar a determinar a causa de uma falha de aplicativo, de inicialização ou de um aplicativo lento.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-802">A *crash dump* is a snapshot of the system's memory and can help determine the cause of an app crash, startup failure, or slow app.</span></span>

#### <a name="app-crashes-or-encounters-an-exception"></a><span data-ttu-id="8024c-803">O aplicativo falha ou encontra uma exceção</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-803">App crashes or encounters an exception</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8024c-804">Obter e analisar um despejo de memória do [WER (Relatório de Erros do Windows)](/windows/desktop/wer/windows-error-reporting):</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-804">Obtain and analyze a dump from [Windows Error Reporting (WER)](/windows/desktop/wer/windows-error-reporting):</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="8024c-805">Crie uma pasta para armazenar os arquivos de despejo de memória em `c:\dumps`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-805">Create a folder to hold crash dump files at `c:\dumps`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8024c-806">O pool de aplicativos deve ter acesso para gravação à pasta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-806">The app pool must have write access to the folder.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="8024c-807">Execute o [script EnableDumps do PowerShell](https://github.com/dotnet/AspNetCore.Docs/blob/master/aspnetcore/test/troubleshoot-azure-iis/scripts/EnableDumps.ps1):</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-807">Run the [EnableDumps PowerShell script](https://github.com/dotnet/AspNetCore.Docs/blob/master/aspnetcore/test/troubleshoot-azure-iis/scripts/EnableDumps.ps1):</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="8024c-808">Se o aplicativo usa o [modelo de hospedagem em processo](xref:host-and-deploy/iis/index#in-process-hosting-model), execute o script para *w3wp.exe* :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-808">If the app uses the [in-process hosting model](xref:host-and-deploy/iis/index#in-process-hosting-model), run the script for *w3wp.exe* :</span></span>

     ```console
     .\EnableDumps w3wp.exe c:\dumps
     ```

   * <span data-ttu-id="8024c-809">Se o aplicativo usa o [modelo de hospedagem fora do processo](xref:host-and-deploy/iis/index#out-of-process-hosting-model), execute o script para *dotnet.exe* :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-809">If the app uses the [out-of-process hosting model](xref:host-and-deploy/iis/index#out-of-process-hosting-model), run the script for *dotnet.exe* :</span></span>

     ```console
     .\EnableDumps dotnet.exe c:\dumps
     ```

1. <span data-ttu-id="8024c-810">Execute o aplicativo sob as condições que causam a falha.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-810">Run the app under the conditions that cause the crash to occur.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="8024c-811">Após a falha, execute o [script DisableDumps do PowerShell](https://github.com/dotnet/AspNetCore.Docs/blob/master/aspnetcore/test/troubleshoot-azure-iis/scripts/DisableDumps.ps1):</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-811">After the crash has occurred, run the [DisableDumps PowerShell script](https://github.com/dotnet/AspNetCore.Docs/blob/master/aspnetcore/test/troubleshoot-azure-iis/scripts/DisableDumps.ps1):</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="8024c-812">Se o aplicativo usa o [modelo de hospedagem em processo](xref:host-and-deploy/iis/index#in-process-hosting-model), execute o script para *w3wp.exe* :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-812">If the app uses the [in-process hosting model](xref:host-and-deploy/iis/index#in-process-hosting-model), run the script for *w3wp.exe* :</span></span>

     ```console
     .\DisableDumps w3wp.exe
     ```

   * <span data-ttu-id="8024c-813">Se o aplicativo usa o [modelo de hospedagem fora do processo](xref:host-and-deploy/iis/index#out-of-process-hosting-model), execute o script para *dotnet.exe* :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-813">If the app uses the [out-of-process hosting model](xref:host-and-deploy/iis/index#out-of-process-hosting-model), run the script for *dotnet.exe* :</span></span>

     ```console
     .\DisableDumps dotnet.exe
     ```

<span data-ttu-id="8024c-814">Depois que um aplicativo falhar e a coleta de despejo de memória for concluída, o aplicativo terá permissão para encerrar normalmente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-814">After an app crashes and dump collection is complete, the app is allowed to terminate normally.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8024c-815">O script do PowerShell configura o WER para coletar até cinco despejos de memória por aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-815">The PowerShell script configures WER to collect up to five dumps per app.</span></span>

> [!WARNING]
> <span data-ttu-id="8024c-816">Os despejos de memória podem usar uma grande quantidade de espaço em disco (até vários gigabytes cada).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-816">Crash dumps might take up a large amount of disk space (up to several gigabytes each).</span></span>

#### <a name="app-hangs-fails-during-startup-or-runs-normally"></a><span data-ttu-id="8024c-817">O aplicativo trava, falha durante a inicialização ou executa normalmente</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-817">App hangs, fails during startup, or runs normally</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8024c-818">Quando um aplicativo *paralisa* (para de responder, mas não falha), falha durante a inicialização ou é executado normalmente, consulte [arquivos de despejo no modo de usuário: escolhendo a melhor ferramenta](/windows-hardware/drivers/debugger/user-mode-dump-files#choosing-the-best-tool) para selecionar uma ferramenta apropriada para produzir o despejo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-818">When an app *hangs* (stops responding but doesn't crash), fails during startup, or runs normally, see [User-Mode Dump Files: Choosing the Best Tool](/windows-hardware/drivers/debugger/user-mode-dump-files#choosing-the-best-tool) to select an appropriate tool to produce the dump.</span></span>

#### <a name="analyze-the-dump"></a><span data-ttu-id="8024c-819">Analisar o despejo de memória</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-819">Analyze the dump</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8024c-820">Um despejo de memória pode ser analisado usando várias abordagens.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-820">A dump can be analyzed using several approaches.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8024c-821">Para obter mais informações, confira [Analisando um arquivo de despejo de memória do modo de usuário](/windows-hardware/drivers/debugger/analyzing-a-user-mode-dump-file).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-821">For more information, see [Analyzing a User-Mode Dump File](/windows-hardware/drivers/debugger/analyzing-a-user-mode-dump-file).</span></span>

## <a name="clear-package-caches"></a><span data-ttu-id="8024c-822">Limpar caches de pacote</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-822">Clear package caches</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8024c-823">Um aplicativo em funcionamento pode falhar imediatamente após a atualização do SDK do .NET Core no computador de desenvolvimento ou a alteração das versões do pacote no aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-823">A functioning app may fail immediately after upgrading either the .NET Core SDK on the development machine or changing package versions within the app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8024c-824">Em alguns casos, pacotes incoerentes podem interromper um aplicativo ao executar atualizações principais.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-824">In some cases, incoherent packages may break an app when performing major upgrades.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8024c-825">A maioria desses problemas pode ser corrigida seguindo estas instruções:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-825">Most of these issues can be fixed by following these instructions:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="8024c-826">Exclua as pastas *bin* e *obj* .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-826">Delete the *bin* and *obj* folders.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="8024c-827">Limpe os caches de pacote executando [dotnet NuGet local All--Clear](/dotnet/core/tools/dotnet-nuget-locals) de um shell de comando.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-827">Clear the package caches by executing [dotnet nuget locals all --clear](/dotnet/core/tools/dotnet-nuget-locals) from a command shell.</span></span>

   <span data-ttu-id="8024c-828">Limpar caches de pacote também pode ser feito com a ferramenta de [nuget.exe](https://www.nuget.org/downloads) e executar o comando `nuget locals all -clear` .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-828">Clearing package caches can also be accomplished with the [nuget.exe](https://www.nuget.org/downloads) tool and executing the command `nuget locals all -clear`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8024c-829">*nuget.exe* não é uma instalação fornecida com o sistema operacional Windows Desktop e devem ser obtidos separadamente do [site do NuGet](https://www.nuget.org/downloads).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-829">*nuget.exe* isn't a bundled install with the Windows desktop operating system and must be obtained separately from the [NuGet website](https://www.nuget.org/downloads).</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="8024c-830">Restaure e recompile o projeto.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-830">Restore and rebuild the project.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="8024c-831">Exclua todos os arquivos na pasta de implantação no servidor antes de reimplantar o aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-831">Delete all of the files in the deployment folder on the server prior to redeploying the app.</span></span>

## <a name="app-startup-errors"></a><span data-ttu-id="8024c-862">Erros de inicialização do aplicativo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-862">App startup errors</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8024c-863">No Visual Studio, um projeto ASP.NET Core usa como padrão a hospedagem [IIS Express](/iis/extensions/introduction-to-iis-express/iis-express-overview) durante a depuração.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-863">In Visual Studio, an ASP.NET Core project defaults to [IIS Express](/iis/extensions/introduction-to-iis-express/iis-express-overview) hosting during debugging.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8024c-864">Uma *falha de processo 502,5* que ocorre ao depurar localmente pode ser diagnosticada usando o Conselho neste tópico.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-864">A *502.5 Process Failure* that occurs when debugging locally can be diagnosed using the advice in this topic.</span></span>

### <a name="40314-forbidden"></a><span data-ttu-id="8024c-865">403,14 proibido</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-865">403.14 Forbidden</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8024c-866">Falha ao iniciar o aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-866">The app fails to start.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8024c-867">O seguinte erro é registrado em log:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-867">The following error is logged:</span></span>

```
The Web server is configured to not list the contents of this directory.
```

<span data-ttu-id="8024c-868">O erro geralmente é causado por uma implantação quebrada no sistema de hospedagem, que inclui qualquer um dos seguintes cenários:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-868">The error is usually caused by a broken deployment on the hosting system, which includes any of the following scenarios:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="8024c-869">O aplicativo é implantado na pasta incorreta no sistema de hospedagem.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-869">The app is deployed to the wrong folder on the hosting system.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="8024c-870">O processo de implantação não moveu todos os arquivos e pastas do aplicativo para a pasta de implantação no sistema de hospedagem.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-870">The deployment process failed to move all of the app's files and folders to the deployment folder on the hosting system.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="8024c-871">O arquivo de *web.config* está ausente na implantação ou o conteúdo do arquivo de *web.config* está malformado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-871">The *web.config* file is missing from the deployment, or the *web.config* file contents are malformed.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8024c-872">Execute as seguintes etapas:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-872">Perform the following steps:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="8024c-873">Exclua todos os arquivos e pastas da pasta de implantação no sistema de hospedagem.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-873">Delete all of the files and folders from the deployment folder on the hosting system.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="8024c-874">Reimplante o conteúdo da pasta de *publicação* do aplicativo no sistema de hospedagem usando o método normal de implantação, como o Visual Studio, o PowerShell ou a implantação manual:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-874">Redeploy the contents of the app's *publish* folder to the hosting system using your normal method of deployment, such as Visual Studio, PowerShell, or manual deployment:</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="8024c-875">Confirme se o arquivo de *web.config* está presente na implantação e se seu conteúdo está correto.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-875">Confirm that the *web.config* file is present in the deployment and that its contents are correct.</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="8024c-876">Ao hospedar no serviço Azure App, confirme se o aplicativo está implantado na `D:\home\site\wwwroot` pasta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-876">When hosting on Azure App Service, confirm that the app is deployed to the `D:\home\site\wwwroot` folder.</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="8024c-877">Quando o aplicativo é hospedado pelo IIS, confirme se o aplicativo está implantado no **caminho físico** do IIS mostrado nas **configurações básicas** do **Gerenciador do IIS** .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-877">When the app is hosted by IIS, confirm that the app is deployed to the IIS **Physical path** shown in **IIS Manager** 's **Basic Settings** .</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="8024c-878">Confirme se todos os arquivos e pastas do aplicativo estão implantados comparando a implantação no sistema de hospedagem ao conteúdo da pasta de *publicação* do projeto.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-878">Confirm that all of the app's files and folders are deployed by comparing the deployment on the hosting system to the contents of the project's *publish* folder.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8024c-879">Para obter mais informações sobre o layout de um aplicativo ASP.NET Core publicado, consulte <xref:host-and-deploy/directory-structure> .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-879">For more information on the layout of a published ASP.NET Core app, see <xref:host-and-deploy/directory-structure>.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8024c-880">Para obter mais informações sobre o arquivo de *web.config* , consulte <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#configuration-with-webconfig> .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-880">For more information on the *web.config* file, see <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#configuration-with-webconfig>.</span></span>

### <a name="500-internal-server-error"></a><span data-ttu-id="8024c-881">Erro interno de servidor 500</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-881">500 Internal Server Error</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8024c-882">O aplicativo é iniciado, mas um erro impede o servidor de atender à solicitação.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-882">The app starts, but an error prevents the server from fulfilling the request.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8024c-883">Esse erro ocorre no código do aplicativo durante a inicialização ou durante a criação de uma resposta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-883">This error occurs within the app's code during startup or while creating a response.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8024c-884">A resposta poderá não conter nenhum conteúdo, ou a resposta poderá ser exibida como um *500 – Erro Interno do Servidor* no navegador.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-884">The response may contain no content, or the response may appear as a *500 Internal Server Error* in the browser.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8024c-885">O Log de Eventos do Aplicativo geralmente indica que o aplicativo iniciou normalmente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-885">The Application Event Log usually states that the app started normally.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8024c-886">Da perspectiva do servidor, isso está correto.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-886">From the server's perspective, that's correct.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8024c-887">O aplicativo foi iniciado, mas não é capaz de gerar uma resposta válida.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-887">The app did start, but it can't generate a valid response.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8024c-888">Execute o aplicativo em um prompt de comando no servidor ou habilite o log de stdout do Módulo do ASP.NET Core para solucionar o problema.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-888">Run the app at a command prompt on the server or enable the ASP.NET Core Module stdout log to troubleshoot the problem.</span></span>

### <a name="5025-process-failure"></a><span data-ttu-id="8024c-889">Falha de processo 502.5</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-889">502.5 Process Failure</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8024c-890">O processo de trabalho falha.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-890">The worker process fails.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8024c-891">O aplicativo não foi iniciado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-891">The app doesn't start.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8024c-892">O [Módulo do ASP.NET Core](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module) tenta iniciar o processo de trabalho, mas falhar ao iniciar.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-892">The [ASP.NET Core Module](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module) attempts to start the worker process but it fails to start.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8024c-893">A causa de uma falha de inicialização do processo geralmente pode ser determinada com base em entradas no Log de Eventos do Aplicativo e no log de stdout do Módulo do ASP.NET Core.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-893">The cause of a process startup failure can usually be determined from entries in the Application Event Log and the ASP.NET Core Module stdout log.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8024c-894">Uma condição de falha comum é o aplicativo configurado incorretamente, direcionado a uma versão da estrutura compartilhada do ASP.NET Core que não está presente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-894">A common failure condition is the app is misconfigured due to targeting a version of the ASP.NET Core shared framework that isn't present.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8024c-895">Verifique quais versões da estrutura compartilhada do ASP.NET Core estão instaladas no computador de destino.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-895">Check which versions of the ASP.NET Core shared framework are installed on the target machine.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8024c-896">A *estrutura compartilhada* é o conjunto de assemblies (arquivos *. dll* ) instalado no computador e referenciado por um metapacote como `Microsoft.AspNetCore.App`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-896">The *shared framework* is the set of assemblies ( *.dll* files) that are installed on the machine and referenced by a metapackage such as `Microsoft.AspNetCore.App`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8024c-897">A referência do metapacote pode especificar a versão mínima necessária.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-897">The metapackage reference can specify a minimum required version.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8024c-898">Saiba mais em [A estrutura compartilhada](https://natemcmaster.com/blog/2018/08/29/netcore-primitives-2/).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-898">For more information, see [The shared framework](https://natemcmaster.com/blog/2018/08/29/netcore-primitives-2/).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8024c-899">A página do erro *502.5 – Falha no Processo* é retornada quando um erro de configuração de hospedagem ou do aplicativo faz com que o processo de trabalho falhe:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-899">The *502.5 Process Failure* error page is returned when a hosting or app misconfiguration causes the worker process to fail:</span></span>

### <a name="failed-to-start-application-errorcode-0x800700c1"></a><span data-ttu-id="8024c-900">Falha ao iniciar o aplicativo (ErrorCode '0x800700c1')</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-900">Failed to start application (ErrorCode '0x800700c1')</span></span>

```
EventID: 1010
Source: IIS AspNetCore Module V2
Failed to start application '/LM/W3SVC/6/ROOT/', ErrorCode '0x800700c1'.
```

<span data-ttu-id="8024c-901">O aplicativo falhou ao ser iniciado porque o assembly do aplicativo ( *.dll* ) não pôde ser carregado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-901">The app failed to start because the app's assembly ( *.dll* ) couldn't be loaded.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8024c-902">Esse erro ocorre quando há uma incompatibilidade de número de bits entre o aplicativo publicado e o processo w3wp/iisexpress.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-902">This error occurs when there's a bitness mismatch between the published app and the w3wp/iisexpress process.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8024c-903">Confirme se a configuração de 32 bits do pool de aplicativos está correta:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-903">Confirm that the app pool's 32-bit setting is correct:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="8024c-904">Selecione o pool de aplicativos no **Pools de Aplicativos** do Gerenciador do IIS.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-904">Select the app pool in IIS Manager's **Application Pools** .</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="8024c-905">Selecione **Configurações Avançadas** em **Editar Pool de Aplicativos** no painel **Ações** .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-905">Select **Advanced Settings** under **Edit Application Pool** in the **Actions** panel.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="8024c-906">Defina **Habilitar Aplicativos de 32 bits** :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-906">Set **Enable 32-Bit Applications** :</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="8024c-907">Se estiver implantando um aplicativo de 32 bits (x86), defina o valor como `True`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-907">If deploying a 32-bit (x86) app, set the value to `True`.</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="8024c-908">Se estiver implantando um aplicativo de 64 bits (x64), defina o valor como `False`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-908">If deploying a 64-bit (x64) app, set the value to `False`.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8024c-909">Confirme se não há um conflito entre uma `<Platform>` Propriedade do MSBuild no arquivo de projeto e o bit de bits publicado do aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-909">Confirm that there isn't a conflict between a `<Platform>` MSBuild property in the project file and the published bitness of the app.</span></span>

### <a name="connection-reset"></a><span data-ttu-id="8024c-910">Redefinição de conexão</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-910">Connection reset</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8024c-911">Se um erro ocorrer após os cabeçalhos serem enviados, será tarde demais para o servidor enviar um **500 – Erro Interno do Servidor** no caso de um erro ocorrer.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-911">If an error occurs after the headers are sent, it's too late for the server to send a **500 Internal Server Error** when an error occurs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8024c-912">Isso geralmente acontece quando ocorre um erro durante a serialização de objetos complexos para uma resposta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-912">This often happens when an error occurs during the serialization of complex objects for a response.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8024c-913">Esse tipo de erro é exibida como um erro de *redefinição de conexão* no cliente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-913">This type of error appears as a *connection reset* error on the client.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8024c-914">O [Log de aplicativo](xref:fundamentals/logging/index) pode ajudar a solucionar esses tipos de erros.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-914">[Application logging](xref:fundamentals/logging/index) can help troubleshoot these types of errors.</span></span>

### <a name="default-startup-limits"></a><span data-ttu-id="8024c-915">Limites de inicialização padrão</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-915">Default startup limits</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8024c-916">O [módulo ASP.NET Core](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module) é configurado com um *startupTimeLimit* padrão de 120 segundos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-916">The [ASP.NET Core Module](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module) is configured with a default *startupTimeLimit* of 120 seconds.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8024c-917">Quando deixado no valor padrão, um aplicativo pode levar até dois minutos para iniciar antes que uma falha do processo seja registrada em log pelo módulo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-917">When left at the default value, an app may take up to two minutes to start before the module logs a process failure.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8024c-918">Para obter informações sobre como configurar o módulo, veja [Atributos do elemento aspNetCore](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#attributes-of-the-aspnetcore-element).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-918">For information on configuring the module, see [Attributes of the aspNetCore element](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#attributes-of-the-aspnetcore-element).</span></span>

## <a name="troubleshoot-on-azure-app-service"></a><span data-ttu-id="8024c-919">Solucionar problemas no serviço Azure App</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-919">Troubleshoot on Azure App Service</span></span>

[!INCLUDE [Azure App Service Preview Notice](~/includes/azure-apps-preview-notice.md)]

### <a name="application-event-log-azure-app-service"></a><span data-ttu-id="8024c-920">Log de eventos do aplicativo (serviço Azure App)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-920">Application Event Log (Azure App Service)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8024c-921">Para acessar o Log de Eventos do Aplicativo, use a folha **Diagnosticar e solucionar problemas** no portal do Azure:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-921">To access the Application Event Log, use the **Diagnose and solve problems** blade in the Azure portal:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="8024c-922">No portal do Azure, abra o aplicativo nos **Serviços de Aplicativos** .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-922">In the Azure portal, open the app in **App Services** .</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="8024c-923">Selecione **Diagnosticar e solucionar problemas** .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-923">Select **Diagnose and solve problems** .</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="8024c-924">Selecione o título **Ferramentas de Diagnóstico** .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-924">Select the **Diagnostic Tools** heading.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="8024c-925">Em **Ferramentas de Suporte** , selecione o botão **Eventos do Aplicativo** .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-925">Under **Support Tools** , select the **Application Events** button.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="8024c-926">Examine o erro mais recente fornecido pela entrada *IIS AspNetCoreModule* ou *IIS AspNetCoreModule V2* na coluna **Origem** .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-926">Examine the latest error provided by the *IIS AspNetCoreModule* or *IIS AspNetCoreModule V2* entry in the **Source** column.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8024c-927">Uma alternativa ao uso da folha **Diagnosticar e resolver problemas** é examinar o arquivo de Log de Eventos do Aplicativo diretamente usando o [Kudu](https://github.com/projectkudu/kudu/wiki):</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-927">An alternative to using the **Diagnose and solve problems** blade is to examine the Application Event Log file directly using [Kudu](https://github.com/projectkudu/kudu/wiki):</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="8024c-928">Abra **Ferramentas Avançadas** na área **Ferramentas de Desenvolvimento** .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-928">Open **Advanced Tools** in the **Development Tools** area.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8024c-929">Selecione o **botão &rarr; ir** .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-929">Select the **Go&rarr;** button.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8024c-930">O console do Kudu é aberto em uma nova janela ou guia do navegador.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-930">The Kudu console opens in a new browser tab or window.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="8024c-931">Usando a barra de navegação na parte superior da página, abra **Console de depuração** e selecione **CMD** .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-931">Using the navigation bar at the top of the page, open **Debug console** and select **CMD** .</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="8024c-932">Abra a pasta **LogFiles** .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-932">Open the **LogFiles** folder.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="8024c-933">Selecione o ícone de lápis ao lado do arquivo *eventlog.xml* .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-933">Select the pencil icon next to the *eventlog.xml* file.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="8024c-934">Examine o log.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-934">Examine the log.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8024c-935">Role até o final do log para ver os eventos mais recentes.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-935">Scroll to the bottom of the log to see the most recent events.</span></span>

### <a name="run-the-app-in-the-kudu-console"></a><span data-ttu-id="8024c-936">Execute o aplicativo no console do Kudu</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-936">Run the app in the Kudu console</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8024c-937">Muitos erros de inicialização não produzem informações úteis no Log de Eventos do Aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-937">Many startup errors don't produce useful information in the Application Event Log.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8024c-938">Você pode executar o aplicativo no Console de Execução Remota do [Kudu](https://github.com/projectkudu/kudu/wiki) para descobrir o erro:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-938">You can run the app in the [Kudu](https://github.com/projectkudu/kudu/wiki) Remote Execution Console to discover the error:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="8024c-939">Abra **Ferramentas Avançadas** na área **Ferramentas de Desenvolvimento** .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-939">Open **Advanced Tools** in the **Development Tools** area.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8024c-940">Selecione o **botão &rarr; ir** .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-940">Select the **Go&rarr;** button.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8024c-941">O console do Kudu é aberto em uma nova janela ou guia do navegador.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-941">The Kudu console opens in a new browser tab or window.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="8024c-942">Usando a barra de navegação na parte superior da página, abra **Console de depuração** e selecione **CMD** .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-942">Using the navigation bar at the top of the page, open **Debug console** and select **CMD** .</span></span>

#### <a name="test-a-32-bit-x86-app"></a><span data-ttu-id="8024c-943">Testar um aplicativo de 32 bits (x86)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-943">Test a 32-bit (x86) app</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8024c-944">**Versão atual**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-944">**Current release**</span></span>

1. `cd d:\home\site\wwwroot`
1. <span data-ttu-id="8024c-945">Executar o aplicativo:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-945">Run the app:</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="8024c-946">Se o aplicativo é uma [implantação dependente de estrutura](/dotnet/core/deploying/#framework-dependent-deployments-fdd):</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-946">If the app is a [framework-dependent deployment](/dotnet/core/deploying/#framework-dependent-deployments-fdd):</span></span>

     ```dotnetcli
     dotnet .\{ASSEMBLY NAME}.dll
     ```

   * <span data-ttu-id="8024c-947">Se o aplicativo é uma [implantação autossuficiente](/dotnet/core/deploying/#self-contained-deployments-scd):</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-947">If the app is a [self-contained deployment](/dotnet/core/deploying/#self-contained-deployments-scd):</span></span>

     ```console
     {ASSEMBLY NAME}.exe
     ```

<span data-ttu-id="8024c-948">A saída do console do aplicativo, mostrando todos os erros, é canalizada para o console do Kudu.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-948">The console output from the app, showing any errors, is piped to the Kudu console.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8024c-949">**Implantação dependente da estrutura em execução em uma versão de visualização**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-949">**Framework-dependent deployment running on a preview release**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8024c-950">*Requer a instalação da extensão de site de runtime do ASP.NET Core {VERSION} (x86).*</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-950">*Requires installing the ASP.NET Core {VERSION} (x86) Runtime site extension.*</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="8024c-951">`cd D:\home\SiteExtensions\AspNetCoreRuntime.{X.Y}.x32` (`{X.Y}` é a versão de runtime)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-951">`cd D:\home\SiteExtensions\AspNetCoreRuntime.{X.Y}.x32` (`{X.Y}` is the runtime version)</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="8024c-952">Execute o aplicativo: `dotnet \home\site\wwwroot\{ASSEMBLY NAME}.dll`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-952">Run the app: `dotnet \home\site\wwwroot\{ASSEMBLY NAME}.dll`</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8024c-953">A saída do console do aplicativo, mostrando todos os erros, é canalizada para o console do Kudu.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-953">The console output from the app, showing any errors, is piped to the Kudu console.</span></span>

#### <a name="test-a-64-bit-x64-app"></a><span data-ttu-id="8024c-954">Testar um aplicativo de 64 bits (x64)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-954">Test a 64-bit (x64) app</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8024c-955">**Versão atual**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-955">**Current release**</span></span>

  1. <span data-ttu-id="8024c-957">Execute o aplicativo: `dotnet \home\site\wwwroot\{ASSEMBLY NAME}.dll`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-957">Run the app: `dotnet \home\site\wwwroot\{ASSEMBLY NAME}.dll`</span></span>

  1. `cd D:\home\site\wwwroot`
  1. <span data-ttu-id="8024c-959">Execute o aplicativo: `{ASSEMBLY NAME}.exe`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-959">Run the app: `{ASSEMBLY NAME}.exe`</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8024c-960">A saída do console do aplicativo, mostrando todos os erros, é canalizada para o console do Kudu.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-960">The console output from the app, showing any errors, is piped to the Kudu console.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8024c-961">**Implantação dependente da estrutura em execução em uma versão de visualização**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-961">**Framework-dependent deployment running on a preview release**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8024c-962">*Requer a instalação da extensão de site de runtime do ASP.NET Core {VERSION} (x64).*</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-962">*Requires installing the ASP.NET Core {VERSION} (x64) Runtime site extension.*</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="8024c-963">`cd D:\home\SiteExtensions\AspNetCoreRuntime.{X.Y}.x64` (`{X.Y}` é a versão de runtime)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8024c-963">`cd D:\home\SiteExtensions\AspNetCoreRuntime.{X.Y}.x64` (`{X.Y}` is the runtime version)</span></span>
